    <script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/monaco-editor/0.45.0/min/vs/loader.min.js"></script>
    
    <script>
        const API_BASE = 'http://localhost:8080/api';
        const LONG_PRESS_DURATION = 500;
        const DRAG_THRESHOLD = 10;
        
        const state = {
            local: {
                currentPath: '/storage/emulated/0',
                files: [],
                selected: null,
                clipboard: null,
                clipboardAction: null
            },
            github: {
                token: localStorage.getItem('gh_token') || '',
                repo: localStorage.getItem('gh_repo') || '',
                currentPath: '',
                files: [],
                selected: null,
                clipboard: null,
                clipboardAction: null,
                connected: false,
                branch: 'main'
            },
            editor: {
                visible: false,
                currentFile: null,
                content: '',
                modified: false
            },
            dropdown: {
                localOpen: false,
                githubOpen: false
            },
            monaco: null,
            editorInstance: null,
            contextMenuTarget: null,
            inputCallback: null
        };

        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
            initMonaco().then(() => {
                setupEventListeners();
                setupResizers();
                setupGlobalTouchHandlers();
                checkServerHealth().then(() => {
                    loadLocalFiles(state.local.currentPath);
                    if (state.github.token && state.github.repo) {
                        document.getElementById('gh-token').value = state.github.token;
                        document.getElementById('gh-repo').value = state.github.repo;
                        connectGitHub(true);
                    }
                });
            });
        });

        function initMonaco() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                require.config({ paths: { 'vs': 'https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/monaco-editor/0.45.0/min/vs' }});
                require(['vs/editor/editor.main'], function() {
                    state.monaco = monaco;
                    state.editorInstance = monaco.editor.create(document.getElementById('monaco-container'), {
                        value: '',
                        language: 'plaintext',
                        theme: 'vs-dark',
                        automaticLayout: true,
                        minimap: { enabled: false },
                        fontSize: 14,
                        fontFamily: 'JetBrains Mono',
                        scrollBeyondLastLine: false,
                        roundedSelection: false,
                        padding: { top: 16 },
                        quickSuggestions: false,
                        suggestOnTriggerCharacters: false,
                        acceptSuggestionOnEnter: 'off',
                        tabCompletion: 'off',
                        wordBasedSuggestions: false,
                        parameterHints: { enabled: false },
                        hover: { enabled: false },
                        formatOnType: false,
                        autoIndent: 'none',
                        dragAndDrop: false
                    });
                    
                    state.editorInstance.onDidChangeCursorPosition((e) => {
                        document.getElementById('editor-cursor').textContent = `Ln ${e.position.lineNumber}, Col ${e.position.column}`;
                    });
                    
                    state.editorInstance.onDidChangeModelContent(() => {
                        if (!state.editor.modified && state.editor.currentFile) {
                            state.editor.modified = true;
                            document.getElementById('editor-dirty').classList.remove('hidden');
                        }
                    });
                    
                    resolve();
                });
            });
        }

        function setupEventListeners() {
            document.getElementById('btn-local-back').addEventListener('click', () => navigateUp('local'));
            document.getElementById('btn-local-refresh').addEventListener('click', () => refreshPanel('local'));
            document.getElementById('btn-local-newfolder').addEventListener('click', () => createFolder('local'));
            
            document.getElementById('btn-github-back').addEventListener('click', () => navigateUp('github'));
            document.getElementById('btn-github-refresh').addEventListener('click', () => refreshPanel('github'));
            document.getElementById('btn-github-newfolder').addEventListener('click', () => createFolder('github'));
            document.getElementById('btn-github-config').addEventListener('click', showGitHubConfig);
            document.getElementById('btn-show-config').addEventListener('click', showGitHubConfig);
            document.getElementById('btn-connect-github').addEventListener('click', () => connectGitHub(false));
            
            document.getElementById('toggle-editor').addEventListener('click', toggleEditor);
            document.getElementById('btn-save-file').addEventListener('click', saveCurrentFile);
            document.getElementById('btn-close-editor').addEventListener('click', closeEditor);
            
            document.getElementById('btn-dropdown-local').addEventListener('click', toggleDropdownLocal);
            document.getElementById('btn-dropdown-github').addEventListener('click', toggleDropdownGithub);
            
            document.getElementById('btn-drop-local-back').addEventListener('click', () => navigateUp('drop-local'));
            document.getElementById('btn-drop-local-close').addEventListener('click', closeDropdownLocal);
            document.getElementById('btn-drop-github-back').addEventListener('click', () => navigateUp('drop-github'));
            document.getElementById('btn-drop-github-close').addEventListener('click', closeDropdownGithub);
            
            document.getElementById('btn-input-cancel').addEventListener('click', closeInputModal);
            document.getElementById('btn-input-ok').addEventListener('click', confirmInput);
            document.getElementById('input-field').addEventListener('keypress', (e) => {
                if (e.key === 'Enter') confirmInput();
            });
            
            document.getElementById('ctx-open').addEventListener('click', () => ctxAction('open'));
            document.getElementById('ctx-edit').addEventListener('click', () => ctxAction('edit'));
            document.getElementById('ctx-copy').addEventListener('click', () => ctxAction('copy'));
            document.getElementById('ctx-cut').addEventListener('click', () => ctxAction('cut'));
            document.getElementById('ctx-paste').addEventListener('click', () => ctxAction('paste'));
            document.getElementById('ctx-rename').addEventListener('click', () => ctxAction('rename'));
            document.getElementById('ctx-delete').addEventListener('click', () => ctxAction('delete'));
            document.getElementById('ctx-transfer').addEventListener('click', () => ctxAction('transfer'));
            
            document.getElementById('menu-overlay').addEventListener('click', hideContextMenu);
            
            document.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
                if (e.ctrlKey || e.metaKey) {
                    if (e.key.toLowerCase() === 's') {
                        e.preventDefault();
                        if (state.editor.visible) saveCurrentFile();
                    }
                }
                if (e.key === 'Escape') {
                    if (state.dropdown.localOpen) closeDropdownLocal();
                    else if (state.dropdown.githubOpen) closeDropdownGithub();
                    else {
                        closeEditor();
                        hideContextMenu();
                        closeInputModal();
                    }
                }
            });
        }

        function setupGlobalTouchHandlers() {
            document.addEventListener('touchmove', function(e) {
                if (e.scale !== 1) e.preventDefault();
            }, { passive: false });
            
            let lastTouchEnd = 0;
            document.addEventListener('touchend', function(e) {
                const now = Date.now();
                if (now - lastTouchEnd <= 300) e.preventDefault();
                lastTouchEnd = now;
            }, false);
        }

        function toggleDropdownLocal() {
            const drop = document.getElementById('dropdown-local');
            const btn = document.getElementById('btn-dropdown-local');
            
            if (state.dropdown.localOpen) {
                closeDropdownLocal();
            } else {
                closeDropdownGithub();
                drop.classList.add('open');
                btn.classList.add('active');
                state.dropdown.localOpen = true;
                renderDropdownFiles('local');
            }
        }

        function closeDropdownLocal() {
            document.getElementById('dropdown-local').classList.remove('open');
            document.getElementById('btn-dropdown-local').classList.remove('active');
            state.dropdown.localOpen = false;
        }

        function toggleDropdownGithub() {
            const drop = document.getElementById('dropdown-github');
            const btn = document.getElementById('btn-dropdown-github');
            
            if (state.dropdown.githubOpen) {
                closeDropdownGithub();
            } else {
                closeDropdownLocal();
                drop.classList.add('open');
                btn.classList.add('active');
                state.dropdown.githubOpen = true;
                renderDropdownFiles('github');
            }
        }

        function closeDropdownGithub() {
            document.getElementById('dropdown-github').classList.remove('open');
            document.getElementById('btn-dropdown-github').classList.remove('active');
            state.dropdown.githubOpen = false;
        }

        function renderDropdownFiles(panel) {
            const isLocal = panel === 'local';
            const files = isLocal ? state.local.files : state.github.files;
            const container = document.getElementById(`drop-${panel}-files`);
            const breadcrumb = document.getElementById(`drop-${panel}-breadcrumb`);
            
            updateBreadcrumbElement(breadcrumb, panel, isLocal ? state.local.currentPath : state.github.currentPath, true);
            
            container.innerHTML = '';
            
            if (files.length === 0) {
                container.innerHTML = `<div class="text-center text-gray-500 mt-8 text-sm p-4"><i class="fas fa-folder-open text-4xl mb-2 opacity-30"></i><p>Empty</p></div>`;
                return;
            }
            
            files.forEach((file, index) => {
                const item = document.createElement('div');
                item.className = 'file-item flex items-center gap-3 p-3 rounded-lg cursor-pointer select-none relative overflow-hidden';
                item.dataset.name = file.name;
                item.dataset.type = file.type;
                
                const icon = getFileIcon(file.name, file.type);
                const size = file.type === 'directory' ? '--' : formatSize(file.size);
                
                item.innerHTML = `
                    <div class="file-icon"><i class="${icon} text-xl ${file.type === 'directory' ? 'text-yellow-500' : 'text-blue-400'}"></i></div>
                    <div class="file-info">
                        <div class="file-name">${file.name}</div>
                        <div class="file-meta">${size} • ${formatDate(file.modified)}</div>
                    </div>
                `;
                
                attachDropdownTouchHandlers(item, panel, file);
                container.appendChild(item);
            });
        }

        function attachDropdownTouchHandlers(item, panel, file) {
            let touchStartTime = 0;
            let hasMoved = false;
            let longPressTimer = null;
            
            function startPress(e) {
                const touch = e.touches ? e.touches[0] : e;
                touchStartTime = Date.now();
                hasMoved = false;
                item.classList.add('pressing');
                
                longPressTimer = setTimeout(() => {
                    if (!hasMoved) {
                        item.classList.remove('pressing');
                        const targetPanel = panel === 'drop-local' ? 'local' : 'github';
                        showContextMenu(e, targetPanel, file);
                    }
                }, LONG_PRESS_DURATION);
            }
            
            function movePress(e) {
                hasMoved = true;
                item.classList.remove('pressing');
                clearTimeout(longPressTimer);
            }
            
            function endPress(e) {
                const duration = Date.now() - touchStartTime;
                item.classList.remove('pressing');
                clearTimeout(longPressTimer);
                
                if (!hasMoved && duration < LONG_PRESS_DURATION) {
                    if (file.type === 'directory') {
                        const targetPanel = panel === 'drop-local' ? 'local' : 'github';
                        const current = targetPanel === 'local' ? state.local.currentPath : state.github.currentPath;
                        const newPath = current ? `${current}/${file.name}` : file.name;
                        
                        if (targetPanel === 'local') {
                            state.local.currentPath = newPath;
                            loadLocalFiles(newPath).then(() => renderDropdownFiles('local'));
                        } else {
                            state.github.currentPath = newPath;
                            loadGitHubFiles(newPath).then(() => renderDropdownFiles('github'));
                        }
                    } else {
                        const targetPanel = panel === 'drop-local' ? 'local' : 'github';
                        transferFile(targetPanel, targetPanel === 'local' ? 'github' : 'local', file);
                    }
                }
            }
            
            item.addEventListener('touchstart', startPress, { passive: true });
            item.addEventListener('touchmove', movePress, { passive: true });
            item.addEventListener('touchend', endPress);
            item.addEventListener('touchcancel', () => {
                item.classList.remove('pressing');
                clearTimeout(longPressTimer);
            });
            
            item.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
                if (file.type === 'directory') {
                    const targetPanel = panel === 'drop-local' ? 'local' : 'github';
                    const current = targetPanel === 'local' ? state.local.currentPath : state.github.currentPath;
                    const newPath = current ? `${current}/${file.name}` : file.name;
                    
                    if (targetPanel === 'local') {
                        state.local.currentPath = newPath;
                        loadLocalFiles(newPath).then(() => renderDropdownFiles('local'));
                    } else {
                        state.github.currentPath = newPath;
                        loadGitHubFiles(newPath).then(() => renderDropdownFiles('github'));
                    }
                }
            });
        }

        function updateBreadcrumbElement(container, panel, path, isDropdown = false) {
            container.innerHTML = '';
            
            if (panel === 'local' || panel === 'drop-local') {
                const basePath = '/storage/emulated/0';
                const parts = path.replace(basePath, '').split('/').filter(p => p);
                let currentPath = basePath;
                
                const root = document.createElement('span');
                root.className = 'breadcrumb-item';
                root.textContent = '/';
                root.onclick = () => {
                    state.local.currentPath = basePath;
                    loadLocalFiles(basePath).then(() => {
                        if (isDropdown) renderDropdownFiles('local');
                    });
                };
                container.appendChild(root);
                
                parts.forEach(part => {
                    const sep = document.createElement('span');
                    sep.className = 'text-gray-600 px-1';
                    sep.textContent = '/';
                    container.appendChild(sep);
                    
                    currentPath += '/' + part;
                    const span = document.createElement('span');
                    span.className = 'breadcrumb-item';
                    span.textContent = part;
                    const snap = currentPath;
                    span.onclick = () => {
                        state.local.currentPath = snap;
                        loadLocalFiles(snap).then(() => {
                            if (isDropdown) renderDropdownFiles('local');
                        });
                    };
                    container.appendChild(span);
                });
            } else {
                const parts = path ? path.split('/').filter(p => p) : [];
                
                const root = document.createElement('span');
                root.className = 'breadcrumb-item text-green-400';
                root.textContent = 'root';
                root.onclick = () => {
                    state.github.currentPath = '';
                    loadGitHubFiles('').then(() => {
                        if (isDropdown) renderDropdownFiles('github');
                    });
                };
                container.appendChild(root);
                
                let currentPath = '';
                parts.forEach(part => {
                    const sep = document.createElement('span');
                    sep.className = 'text-gray-600 px-1';
                    sep.textContent = '/';
                    container.appendChild(sep);
                    
                    currentPath = currentPath ? `${currentPath}/${part}` : part;
                    const span = document.createElement('span');
                    span.className = 'breadcrumb-item text-green-400';
                    span.textContent = part;
                    const snap = currentPath;
                    span.onclick = () => {
                        state.github.currentPath = snap;
                        loadGitHubFiles(snap).then(() => {
                            if (isDropdown) renderDropdownFiles('github');
                        });
                    };
                    container.appendChild(span);
                });
            }
        }

        async function checkServerHealth() {
            try {
                const response = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/health`);
                const data = await response.json();
                updateServerStatus(data.status === 'ok' ? 'connected' : 'error', data.status === 'ok' ? 'Connected' : 'Error');
            } catch (err) {
                updateServerStatus('error', 'Offline');
                showNotification('Server offline', 'error', 3000);
            }
        }

        function updateServerStatus(status, text) {
            const indicator = document.getElementById('server-status');
            const statusText = document.getElementById('status-text');
            const colors = { connected: 'bg-green-500', error: 'bg-red-500', connecting: 'bg-yellow-500' };
            indicator.className = `w-2 h-2 rounded-full ${colors[status] || 'bg-gray-500'} status-pulse`;
            statusText.textContent = text;
        }

        async function loadLocalFiles(path) {
            showLoading('local', true);
            try {
                const response = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/local/list?path=${encodeURIComponent(path)}`);
                const data = await response.json();
                if (!data.success) throw new Error(data.error);
                state.local.files = data.files;
                state.local.currentPath = path;
                renderFileList('local', data.files);
                updateBreadcrumbElement(document.getElementById('local-breadcrumb'), 'local', path);
                document.getElementById('local-count').textContent = `${data.files.length} items`;
                document.getElementById('local-path').textContent = path;
            } catch (error) {
                showNotification(`Error: ${error.message}`, 'error');
            } finally {
                showLoading('local', false);
            }
        }

        async function loadGitHubFiles(path = '') {
            if (!state.github.connected) return;
            showLoading('github', true);
            try {
                const response = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/github/list?path=${encodeURIComponent(path)}`);
                const data = await response.json();
                if (!data.success) throw new Error(data.error);
                state.github.files = data.files;
                state.github.currentPath = path;
                renderFileList('github', data.files);
                updateBreadcrumbElement(document.getElementById('github-breadcrumb'), 'github', path);
                document.getElementById('github-count').textContent = `${data.files.length} items`;
            } catch (error) {
                showNotification(`Error: ${error.message}`, 'error');
            } finally {
                showLoading('github', false);
            }
        }

        function renderFileList(panel, files) {
            const container = document.getElementById(`${panel}-files`);
            container.innerHTML = '';
            
            if (files.length === 0) {
                container.innerHTML = `<div class="text-center text-gray-500 mt-8 text-sm p-4"><i class="fas fa-folder-open text-4xl mb-2 opacity-30"></i><p>Empty</p></div>`;
                return;
            }
            
            files.forEach((file, index) => {
                const item = document.createElement('div');
                item.className = 'file-item flex items-center gap-3 p-3 rounded-lg cursor-pointer select-none relative overflow-hidden';
                if (!("ontouchstart" in window)) { item.draggable = true; }
                item.dataset.name = file.name;
                item.dataset.type = file.type;
                item.dataset.index = index;
                item.dataset.path = file.path || '';
                
                const icon = getFileIcon(file.name, file.type);
                const size = file.type === 'directory' ? '--' : formatSize(file.size);
                
                item.innerHTML = `
                    <div class="file-icon"><i class="${icon} text-xl ${file.type === 'directory' ? 'text-yellow-500' : 'text-blue-400'}"></i></div>
                    <div class="file-info">
                        <div class="file-name">${file.name}</div>
                        <div class="file-meta">${size} • ${formatDate(file.modified)}</div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="long-press-indicator"></div>
                `;
                
                attachTouchHandlers(item, panel, file, index);
                container.appendChild(item);
            });
        }

        function attachTouchHandlers(item, panel, file, index) {
            let touchStartX = 0;
            let touchStartY = 0;
            let touchStartTime = 0;
            let longPressTimer = null;
            let hasMoved = false;
            
            function startPress(e) {
                const touch = e.touches ? e.touches[0] : e;
                touchStartX = touch.clientX;
                touchStartY = touch.clientY;
                touchStartTime = Date.now();
                hasMoved = false;
                item.classList.add('pressing');
                
                longPressTimer = setTimeout(() => {
                    if (!hasMoved) {
                        item.classList.remove('pressing');
                        showContextMenu(e, panel, file);
                    }
                }, LONG_PRESS_DURATION);
            }
            
            function movePress(e) {
                if (!touchStartTime) return;
                const touch = e.touches ? e.touches[0] : e;
                const deltaX = Math.abs(touch.clientX - touchStartX);
                const deltaY = Math.abs(touch.clientY - touchStartY);
                
                if (deltaX > DRAG_THRESHOLD || deltaY > DRAG_THRESHOLD) {
                    hasMoved = true;
                    item.classList.remove('pressing');
                    clearTimeout(longPressTimer);
                }
            }
            
            function endPress(e) {
                const duration = Date.now() - touchStartTime;
                item.classList.remove('pressing');
                clearTimeout(longPressTimer);
                
                if (!hasMoved && duration < LONG_PRESS_DURATION) {
                    if (file.type === 'directory') {
                        openFile(panel, file);
                    } else {
                        selectFile(panel, index, e);
                        setTimeout(() => openFile(panel, file), 50);
                    }
                }
                touchStartTime = 0;
            }
            
            item.addEventListener('touchstart', startPress, { passive: true });
            item.addEventListener('touchmove', movePress, { passive: true });
            item.addEventListener('touchend', endPress);
            item.addEventListener('touchcancel', () => {
                item.classList.remove('pressing');
                clearTimeout(longPressTimer);
                touchStartTime = 0;
            });
            
            item.addEventListener('mousedown', (e) => {
                if (e.button === 2) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    showContextMenu(e, panel, file);
                }
            });
            
            item.addEventListener('contextmenu', (e) => {
                e.preventDefault();
                showContextMenu(e, panel, file);
            });
            
            item.addEventListener('dragstart', (e) => handleDragStart(e, panel, file));
            item.addEventListener('dragend', handleDragEnd);
            
            item.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
                e.stopPropagation();
                selectFile(panel, index, e);
            });
            
            item.addEventListener('dblclick', (e) => {
                e.stopPropagation();
                openFile(panel, file);
            });
        }

        function getFileIcon(name, type) {
            if (type === 'directory') return 'fas fa-folder';
            const ext = name.split('.').pop().toLowerCase();
            const icons = {
                'js': 'fab fa-js text-yellow-400',
                'html': 'fab fa-html5 text-orange-500',
                'css': 'fab fa-css3 text-blue-500',
                'json': 'fas fa-code text-gray-400',
                'md': 'fas fa-markdown text-white',
                'txt': 'fas fa-file-alt text-gray-400',
                'py': 'fab fa-python text-blue-300',
                'java': 'fab fa-java text-red-400',
                'png': 'fas fa-image text-purple-400',
                'jpg': 'fas fa-image text-purple-400',
                'pdf': 'fas fa-file-pdf text-red-500',
                'zip': 'fas fa-file-archive text-yellow-600'
            };
            return icons[ext] || 'fas fa-file text-gray-400';
        }

        function formatSize(bytes) {
            if (!bytes) return '0 B';
            const k = 1024;
            const sizes = ['B', 'KB', 'MB', 'GB'];
            const i = Math.floor(Math.log(bytes) / Math.log(k));
            return parseFloat((bytes / Math.pow(k, i)).toFixed(1)) + ' ' + sizes[i];
        }

        function formatDate(dateStr) {
            if (!dateStr) return 'Unknown';
            return new Date(dateStr).toLocaleDateString();
        }

        function navigateTo(panel, path) {
            if (panel === 'local' || panel === 'drop-local') loadLocalFiles(path);
            else loadGitHubFiles(path);
        }

        function navigateUp(panel) {
            if (panel === 'local' || panel === 'drop-local') {
                const current = state.local.currentPath;
                if (current === '/storage/emulated/0') return;
                const parent = current.substring(0, current.lastIndexOf('/')) || '/storage/emulated/0';
                loadLocalFiles(parent);
            } else {
                const current = state.github.currentPath;
                if (!current) return;
                const lastSlash = current.lastIndexOf('/');
                const parent = lastSlash > 0 ? current.substring(0, lastSlash) : '';
                loadGitHubFiles(parent);
            }
        }

        function refreshPanel(panel) {
            if (panel === 'local') loadLocalFiles(state.local.currentPath);
            else loadGitHubFiles(state.github.currentPath);
        }

        function selectFile(panel, index, event) {
            const container = document.getElementById(`${panel}-files`);
            const items = container.querySelectorAll('.file-item');
            items.forEach(i => i.classList.remove('selected'));
            items[index].classList.add('selected');
            
            if (panel === 'local') state.local.selected = state.local.files[index];
            else state.github.selected = state.github.files[index];
        }

        async function openFile(panel, file) {
            if (file.type === 'directory') {
                let newPath;
                if (panel === 'local') {
                    const current = state.local.currentPath;
                    newPath = current.endsWith('/') ? `${current}${file.name}` : `${current}/${file.name}`;
                } else {
                    const current = state.github.currentPath;
                    newPath = current ? `${current}/${file.name}` : file.name;
                }
                navigateTo(panel, newPath);
                return;
            }
            
            const textExts = ['txt', 'md', 'js', 'html', 'css', 'json', 'py', 'java', 'c', 'cpp', 'go', 'rs', 'ts', 'xml', 'yaml', 'yml'];
            const ext = file.name.split('.').pop().toLowerCase();
            
            if (!textExts.includes(ext)) {
                showNotification('Binary file', 'warning');
                return;
            }
            
            openEditor(panel, file);
        }

        async function openEditor(panel, file) {
            try {
                let content = '';
                if (panel === 'local') {
                    content = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/local/read?path=${encodeURIComponent(state.local.currentPath + '/' + file.name)}`).then(r => r.text());
                } else {
                    const data = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/github/read?path=${encodeURIComponent(file.path || file.name)}`).then(r => r.json());
                    content = data.content;
                }
                
                state.editor.currentFile = { panel, file, originalContent: content };
                state.editor.visible = true;
                state.editor.modified = false;
                
                document.getElementById('editor-filename').textContent = file.name;
                document.getElementById('editor-dirty').classList.add('hidden');
                
                document.getElementById('left-panel').style.display = 'none';
                document.getElementById('right-panel').style.display = 'none';
                document.getElementById('resizer-1').style.display = 'none';
                document.getElementById('main-header').style.display = 'none';
                
                const editorPanel = document.getElementById('editor-panel');
                editorPanel.style.width = '100%';
                editorPanel.classList.add('active');
                
                if (state.editorInstance) {
                    const lang = getLanguage(file.name);
                    state.monaco.editor.setModelLanguage(state.editorInstance.getModel(), lang);
                    state.editorInstance.setValue(content);
                    document.getElementById('editor-lang').textContent = lang;
                }
            } catch (error) {
                showNotification(`Error: ${error.message}`, 'error');
            }
        }

        function closeEditor() {
            if (state.editor.modified && !confirm('Discard changes?')) return;
            
            state.editor.visible = false;
            state.editor.currentFile = null;
            state.editor.modified = false;
            
            closeDropdownLocal();
            closeDropdownGithub();
            
            document.getElementById('editor-panel').classList.remove('active');
            
            document.getElementById('left-panel').style.display = 'flex';
            document.getElementById('right-panel').style.display = 'flex';
            document.getElementById('resizer-1').style.display = 'block';
            document.getElementById('main-header').style.display = 'flex';
        }

        function toggleEditor() {
            if (state.editor.visible) closeEditor();
            else if (state.editor.currentFile) openEditor(state.editor.currentFile.panel, state.editor.currentFile.file);
        }

        async function saveCurrentFile() {
            if (!state.editor.currentFile) return;
            
            const { panel, file } = state.editor.currentFile;
            const content = state.editorInstance.getValue();
            
            try {
                if (panel === 'local') {
                    await fetch(`${API_BASE}/local/write`, {
                        method: 'POST',
                        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                        body: JSON.stringify({ path: state.local.currentPath + '/' + file.name, content })
                    });
                } else {
                    await fetch(`${API_BASE}/github/update`, {
                        method: 'POST',
                        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                        body: JSON.stringify({ path: file.path || file.name, content, sha: file.sha })
                    });
                    await loadGitHubFiles(state.github.currentPath);
                }
                
                state.editor.modified = false;
                document.getElementById('editor-dirty').classList.add('hidden');
                showNotification('Saved', 'success');
            } catch (error) {
                showNotification(`Error: ${error.message}`, 'error');
            }
        }

        function getLanguage(filename) {
            const ext = filename.split('.').pop().toLowerCase();
            const langs = { js: 'javascript', ts: 'typescript', html: 'html', css: 'css', json: 'json', md: 'markdown', py: 'python', java: 'java', cpp: 'cpp', c: 'c', go: 'go', rs: 'rust', xml: 'xml', yaml: 'yaml', yml: 'yaml' };
            return langs[ext] || 'plaintext';
        }

        function handleDragStart(e, panel, file) {
            e.target.classList.add('dragging');
            e.dataTransfer.effectAllowed = 'copy';
            e.dataTransfer.setData('application/json', JSON.stringify({ panel, file }));
        }

        function handleDragEnd(e) {
            e.target.classList.remove('dragging');
        }

        function setupResizers() {
            const resizer1 = document.getElementById('resizer-1');
            const leftPanel = document.getElementById('left-panel');
            
            let isResizing = false;
            
            function initResize(e) {
                isResizing = true;
                resizer1.classList.add('active');
                e.preventDefault();
            }
            
            resizer1.addEventListener('mousedown', initResize);
            resizer1.addEventListener('touchstart', initResize, { passive: false });
            
            document.addEventListener('mousemove', (e) => {
                if (!isResizing) return;
                const width = Math.max(200, Math.min(e.clientX, window.innerWidth * 0.7));
                leftPanel.style.width = width + 'px';
            });
            
            document.addEventListener('touchmove', (e) => {
                if (!isResizing) return;
                const width = Math.max(200, Math.min(e.touches[0].clientX, window.innerWidth * 0.7));
                leftPanel.style.width = width + 'px';
            }, { passive: false });
            
            document.addEventListener('mouseup', () => { isResizing = false; resizer1.classList.remove('active'); });
            document.addEventListener('touchend', () => { isResizing = false; resizer1.classList.remove('active'); });
            
            ['local-files', 'github-files'].forEach(id => {
                const container = document.getElementById(id);
                const targetPanel = id === 'local-files' ? 'local' : 'github';
                
                container.addEventListener('dragover', (e) => { e.preventDefault(); e.dataTransfer.dropEffect = 'copy'; });
                container.addEventListener('drop', async (e) => {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    const data = e.dataTransfer.getData('application/json');
                    if (!data) return;
                    const { panel: sourcePanel, file } = JSON.parse(data);
                    if (sourcePanel !== targetPanel) await transferFile(sourcePanel, targetPanel, file);
                });
            });
        }

        async function transferFile(from, to, file) {
            if (file.type === 'directory') {
                showNotification('Folders not supported', 'warning');
                return;
            }
            
            showTransferProgress(true, `Transferring ${file.name}...`);
            
            try {
                if (from === 'local' && to === 'github') {
                    await fetch(`${API_BASE}/transfer/local-to-github`, {
                        method: 'POST',
                        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                        body: JSON.stringify({
                            localPath: state.local.currentPath + '/' + file.name,
                            githubPath: state.github.currentPath ? state.github.currentPath + '/' + file.name : file.name
                        })
                    });
                } else if (from === 'github' && to === 'local') {
                    await fetch(`${API_BASE}/transfer/github-to-local`, {
                        method: 'POST',
                        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                        body: JSON.stringify({
                            githubPath: file.path || file.name,
                            localPath: state.local.currentPath + '/' + file.name
                        })
                    });
                }
                
                showTransferProgress(false);
                showNotification('Transferred', 'success');
                refreshPanel(to);
            } catch (error) {
                showTransferProgress(false);
                showNotification(`Error: ${error.message}`, 'error');
            }
        }

        function showContextMenu(e, panel, file) {
            state.contextMenuTarget = { panel, file };
            
            const menu = document.getElementById('context-menu');
            const overlay = document.getElementById('menu-overlay');
            const header = document.getElementById('ctx-header');
            
            header.textContent = file.name;
            
            const x = Math.min(e.clientX || e.touches?.[0]?.clientX || 100, window.innerWidth - 220);
            const y = Math.min(e.clientY || e.touches?.[0]?.clientY || 100, window.innerHeight - 350);
            
            menu.style.left = x + 'px';
            menu.style.top = y + 'px';
            menu.classList.remove('hidden');
            overlay.classList.add('active');
        }

        function hideContextMenu() {
            document.getElementById('context-menu').classList.add('hidden');
            document.getElementById('menu-overlay').classList.remove('active');
        }

        async function ctxAction(action) {
            const { panel, file } = state.contextMenuTarget;
            hideContextMenu();
            
            switch(action) {
                case 'open':
                case 'edit':
                    await openFile(panel, file);
                    break;
                case 'copy':
                    if (panel === 'local') { state.local.clipboard = file; state.local.clipboardAction = 'copy'; }
                    else { state.github.clipboard = file; state.github.clipboardAction = 'copy'; }
                    showNotification('Copied', 'info');
                    break;
                case 'cut':
                    if (panel === 'local') { state.local.clipboard = file; state.local.clipboardAction = 'cut'; }
                    else { state.github.clipboard = file; state.github.clipboardAction = 'cut'; }
                    showNotification('Cut', 'info');
                    break;
                case 'paste':
                    await handlePaste(panel);
                    break;
                case 'rename':
                    const newName = prompt('New name:', file.name);
                    if (newName && newName !== file.name) {
                        try {
                            if (panel === 'local') {
                                await fetch(`${API_BASE}/local/rename`, {
                                    method: 'POST',
                                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                                    body: JSON.stringify({ oldPath: state.local.currentPath + '/' + file.name, newPath: state.local.currentPath + '/' + newName })
                                });
                                refreshPanel('local');
                            }
                        } catch (error) {
                            showNotification(`Error: ${error.message}`, 'error');
                        }
                    }
                    break;
                case 'delete':
                    if (!confirm(`Delete "${file.name}"?`)) return;
                    try {
                        if (panel === 'local') {
                            await fetch(`${API_BASE}/local/delete`, {
                                method: 'POST',
                                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                                body: JSON.stringify({ path: state.local.currentPath + '/' + file.name })
                            });
                            refreshPanel('local');
                        } else {
                            await fetch(`${API_BASE}/github/delete`, {
                                method: 'POST',
                                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                                body: JSON.stringify({ path: file.path || file.name, sha: file.sha, message: `Delete ${file.name}` })
                            });
                            refreshPanel('github');
                        }
                        showNotification('Deleted', 'success');
                    } catch (error) {
                        showNotification(`Error: ${error.message}`, 'error');
                    }
                    break;
                case 'transfer':
                    await transferFile(panel, panel === 'local' ? 'github' : 'local', file);
                    break;
            }
        }

        async function handlePaste(panel) {
            const clipboard = panel === 'local' ? state.local.clipboard : state.github.clipboard;
            if (!clipboard) { showNotification('Clipboard empty', 'warning'); return; }
            
            if (panel === 'local' && state.local.clipboardAction === 'copy') {
                try {
                    const content = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/local/read?path=${encodeURIComponent(state.local.currentPath + '/' + clipboard.name)}`).then(r => r.text());
                    await fetch(`${API_BASE}/local/write`, {
                        method: 'POST',
                        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                        body: JSON.stringify({ path: state.local.currentPath + '/' + clipboard.name + '_copy', content })
                    });
                    refreshPanel('local');
                    showNotification('Pasted', 'success');
                } catch (error) {
                    showNotification(`Error: ${error.message}`, 'error');
                }
            }
        }

        function createFolder(panel) {
            state.inputCallback = async (name) => {
                if (!name) return;
                try {
                    if (panel === 'local') {
                        await fetch(`${API_BASE}/local/mkdir`, {
                            method: 'POST',
                            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                            body: JSON.stringify({ path: state.local.currentPath + '/' + name })
                        });
                        refreshPanel('local');
                    } else {
                        await fetch(`${API_BASE}/github/create`, {
                            method: 'POST',
                            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                            body: JSON.stringify({ path: (state.github.currentPath ? state.github.currentPath + '/' : '') + name + '/.gitkeep', content: '' })
                        });
                        refreshPanel('github');
                    }
                    showNotification('Created', 'success');
                } catch (error) {
                    showNotification(`Error: ${error.message}`, 'error');
                }
            };
            showInputModal('New Folder', 'Enter name:');
        }

        function showLoading(panel, show) {
            document.getElementById(`${panel}-files`).style.opacity = show ? '0.5' : '1';
        }

        function showTransferProgress(show, text) {
            const modal = document.getElementById('transfer-modal');
            const progress = document.getElementById('transfer-progress');
            
            if (show) {
                modal.classList.remove('hidden');
                modal.classList.add('flex');
                document.getElementById('transfer-text').textContent = text;
                progress.style.width = '30%';
                setTimeout(() => progress.style.width = '70%', 200);
            } else {
                progress.style.width = '100%';
                setTimeout(() => {
                    modal.classList.add('hidden');
                    modal.classList.remove('flex');
                    progress.style.width = '0%';
                }, 300);
            }
        }

        function showInputModal(title, placeholder) {
            document.getElementById('input-title').textContent = title;
            document.getElementById('input-field').placeholder = placeholder;
            document.getElementById('input-field').value = '';
            document.getElementById('input-modal').classList.remove('hidden');
            document.getElementById('input-modal').classList.add('flex');
            document.getElementById('input-field').focus();
        }

        function closeInputModal() {
            document.getElementById('input-modal').classList.add('hidden');
            document.getElementById('input-modal').classList.remove('flex');
            state.inputCallback = null;
        }

        function confirmInput() {
            const value = document.getElementById('input-field').value;
            if (state.inputCallback) state.inputCallback(value);
            closeInputModal();
        }

        function showNotification(message, type = 'info', duration = 3000) {
            const container = document.getElementById('notifications');
            const div = document.createElement('div');
            
            const colors = { success: 'bg-green-600', error: 'bg-red-600', warning: 'bg-yellow-600', info: 'bg-blue-600' };
            const icons = { success: 'fa-check-circle', error: 'fa-exclamation-circle', warning: 'fa-exclamation-triangle', info: 'fa-info-circle' };
            
            div.className = `notification ${colors[type]} text-white px-4 py-3 rounded-lg shadow-lg flex items-center gap-3 pointer-events-auto`;
            div.innerHTML = `<i class="fas ${icons[type]}"></i><span class="flex-1">${message}</span>`;
            
            container.appendChild(div);
            setTimeout(() => {
                div.style.opacity = '0';
                div.style.transform = 'translateX(100%)';
                setTimeout(() => div.remove(), 300);
            }, duration);
        }

        function showGitHubConfig() {
            document.getElementById('github-config').classList.toggle('hidden');
        }

        async function connectGitHub(silent = false) {
            const token = document.getElementById('gh-token').value;
            const repo = document.getElementById('gh-repo').value;
            
            if (!token || !repo) {
                if (!silent) showNotification('Enter token and repo', 'error');
                return;
            }
            
            try {
                const response = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/github/connect`, {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                    body: JSON.stringify({ token, repo })
                });
                
                const data = await response.json();
                
                if (data.success) {
                    state.github.connected = true;
                    state.github.token = token;
                    state.github.repo = repo;
                    localStorage.setItem('gh_token', token);
                    localStorage.setItem('gh_repo', repo);
                    
                    document.getElementById('github-config').classList.add('hidden');
                    showNotification('Connected', 'success');
                    await loadGitHubFiles('');
                } else {
                    throw new Error(data.error);
                }
            } catch (error) {
                showNotification(`Error: ${error.message}`, 'error');
                state.github.connected = false;
            }
        }
    </script>
</body>
</html>

            </div>

            </div>
