    </div>

    <!-- Context Menu -->
    <div id="context-menu" class="context-menu fixed bg-gray-800 border border-gray-700 rounded shadow-xl py-1 hidden z-50 min-w-[160px]">
        <div class="px-3 py-1 text-xs text-gray-500 font-medium border-b border-gray-700 mb-1" id="ctx-header">Actions</div>
        <button class="w-full text-left px-4 py-2 text-sm hover:bg-gray-700 flex items-center gap-2" onclick="ctxAction('open')">
            <i class="fas fa-external-link-alt text-blue-400 w-4"></i> Open
        </button>
        <button class="w-full text-left px-4 py-2 text-sm hover:bg-gray-700 flex items-center gap-2" onclick="ctxAction('copy')">
            <i class="fas fa-copy text-gray-400 w-4"></i> Copy
        </button>
        <button class="w-full text-left px-4 py-2 text-sm hover:bg-gray-700 flex items-center gap-2" onclick="ctxAction('cut')">
            <i class="fas fa-cut text-gray-400 w-4"></i> Cut
        </button>
        <button class="w-full text-left px-4 py-2 text-sm hover:bg-gray-700 flex items-center gap-2" onclick="ctxAction('paste')">
            <i class="fas fa-paste text-green-400 w-4"></i> Paste
        </button>
        <div class="border-t border-gray-700 my-1"></div>
        <button class="w-full text-left px-4 py-2 text-sm hover:bg-gray-700 flex items-center gap-2" onclick="ctxAction('rename')">
            <i class="fas fa-edit text-yellow-400 w-4"></i> Rename
        </button>
        <button class="w-full text-left px-4 py-2 text-sm hover:bg-gray-700 flex items-center gap-2" onclick="ctxAction('delete')">
            <i class="fas fa-trash text-red-400 w-4"></i> Delete
        </button>
        <div class="border-t border-gray-700 my-1"></div>
        <button class="w-full text-left px-4 py-2 text-sm hover:bg-gray-700 flex items-center gap-2" onclick="ctxAction('transfer')">
            <i class="fas fa-exchange-alt text-purple-400 w-4"></i> Transfer to Other Panel
        </button>
    </div>

    <!-- Transfer Progress Modal -->
    <div id="transfer-modal" class="fixed inset-0 bg-black bg-opacity-50 hidden items-center justify-center z-50">
        <div class="bg-gray-800 rounded-lg p-6 w-96 border border-gray-700 shadow-2xl">
            <div class="flex items-center gap-3 mb-4">
                <div class="spinner"></div>
                <span class="font-medium" id="transfer-text">Transferring...</span>
            </div>
            <div class="w-full bg-gray-700 rounded-full h-2">
                <div id="transfer-progress" class="bg-blue-500 h-2 rounded-full transition-all" style="width: 0%"></div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>

    <!-- Input Modal -->
    <div id="input-modal" class="fixed inset-0 bg-black bg-opacity-50 hidden items-center justify-center z-50">
        <div class="bg-gray-800 rounded-lg p-6 w-96 border border-gray-700 shadow-2xl">
            <h3 class="text-lg font-medium mb-4" id="input-title">New Folder</h3>
            <input type="text" id="input-field" class="w-full bg-gray-900 border border-gray-700 rounded px-3 py-2 mb-4 text-white focus:outline-none focus:border-blue-500" placeholder="Name...">
            <div class="flex justify-end gap-2">
                <button onclick="closeInputModal()" class="px-4 py-2 text-gray-400 hover:text-white">Cancel</button>
                <button onclick="confirmInput()" class="px-4 py-2 bg-blue-600 hover:bg-blue-500 rounded text-white font-medium">OK</button>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        // State Management
        const state = {
            local: {
                currentPath: '/storage/emulated/0',
                files: [],
                selected: null,
                clipboard: null,
                clipboardAction: null
            },
            github: {
                token: localStorage.getItem('gh_token') || '',
                repo: localStorage.getItem('gh_repo') || '',
                currentPath: '',
                files: [],
                selected: null,
                clipboard: null,
                clipboardAction: null,
                branch: 'main'
            },
            editor: {
                visible: false,
                currentFile: null,
                content: '',
                modified: false
            },
            monaco: null,
            editorInstance: null
        };

        // Mock Data for Demo (Replace with actual API calls)
        const mockLocalFiles = {
            '/storage/emulated/0': [
                { name: 'Documents', type: 'directory', size: 0, modified: '2024-01-15' },
                { name: 'Downloads', type: 'directory', size: 0, modified: '2024-01-14' },
                { name: 'Pictures', type: 'directory', size: 0, modified: '2024-01-13' },
                { name: 'config.json', type: 'file', size: 1024, modified: '2024-01-12' },
                { name: 'readme.txt', type: 'file', size: 512, modified: '2024-01-11' }
            ],
            '/storage/emulated/0/Documents': [
                { name: 'Work', type: 'directory', size: 0, modified: '2024-01-10' },
                { name: 'Personal', type: 'directory', size: 0, modified: '2024-01-09' },
                { name: 'notes.md', type: 'file', size: 2048, modified: '2024-01-08' }
            ]
        };

        // Initialize
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
            initMonaco();
            loadLocalFiles(state.local.currentPath);
            setupResizers();
            setupDragAndDrop();
            setupKeyboardShortcuts();
            
            // Load saved GitHub config
            if (state.github.token && state.github.repo) {
                document.getElementById('gh-token').value = state.github.token;
                document.getElementById('gh-repo').value = state.github.repo;
                loadGitHubFiles('');
            }
        });

        // Monaco Editor Initialization
        function initMonaco() {
            require.config({ paths: { 'vs': 'https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/monaco-editor/0.45.0/min/vs' }});
            require(['vs/editor/editor.main'], function() {
                state.monaco = monaco;
                state.editorInstance = monaco.editor.create(document.getElementById('monaco-container'), {
                    value: '',
                    language: 'plaintext',
                    theme: 'vs-dark',
                    automaticLayout: true,
                    minimap: { enabled: false },
                    fontSize: 14,
                    fontFamily: 'JetBrains Mono',
                    scrollBeyondLastLine: false,
                    roundedSelection: false,
                    padding: { top: 16 }
                });
                
                state.editorInstance.onDidChangeCursorPosition((e) => {
                    document.getElementById('editor-cursor').textContent = `Ln ${e.position.lineNumber}, Col ${e.position.column}`;
                });
                
                state.editorInstance.onDidChangeModelContent(() => {
                    state.editor.modified = true;
                    document.getElementById('editor-filename').classList.add('text-yellow-400');
                });
            });
        }

        // File Operations
        async function loadLocalFiles(path) {
            showLoading('local', true);
            
            // Simulate API call - Replace with actual fetch to your backend
            setTimeout(() => {
                const files = mockLocalFiles[path] || generateMockFiles(path);
                state.local.files = files;
                state.local.currentPath = path;
                renderFileList('local', files);
                updateBreadcrumb('local', path);
                document.getElementById('local-count').textContent = `${files.length} items`;
                document.getElementById('local-path').textContent = path;
                showLoading('local', false);
            }, 200);
        }

        async function loadGitHubFiles(path) {
            if (!state.github.token || !state.github.repo) {
                document.getElementById('github-files').innerHTML = `
                    <div class="text-center text-gray-500 mt-8 text-sm">
                        <i class="fas fa-key text-4xl mb-2 opacity-50"></i>
                        <p>Please configure GitHub token and repository</p>
                    </div>
                `;
                return;
            }
            
            showLoading('github', true);
            
            // GitHub API Implementation
            try {
                const response = await fetch(`https://api.github.com/repos/${state.github.repo}/contents/${path}?ref=${state.github.branch}`, {
                    headers: {
                        'Authorization': `token ${state.github.token}`,
                        'Accept': 'application/vnd.github.v3+json'
                    }
                });
                
                if (!response.ok) throw new Error('Failed to fetch');
                
                const data = await response.json();
                const files = Array.isArray(data) ? data : [data];
                
                state.github.files = files.map(f => ({
                    name: f.name,
                    type: f.type === 'dir' ? 'directory' : 'file',
                    size: f.size || 0,
                    sha: f.sha,
                    path: f.path,
                    download_url: f.download_url
                }));
                
                state.github.currentPath = path;
                renderFileList('github', state.github.files);
                updateBreadcrumb('github', path);
                document.getElementById('github-count').textContent = `${state.github.files.length} items`;
            } catch (err) {
                showNotification('Error loading GitHub: ' + err.message, 'error');
            } finally {
                showLoading('github', false);
            }
        }

        function renderFileList(panel, files) {
            const container = document.getElementById(`${panel}-files`);
            container.innerHTML = '';
            
            files.forEach((file, index) => {
                const item = document.createElement('div');
                item.className = 'file-item flex items-center gap-3 px-3 py-2 rounded cursor-pointer select-none';
                item.draggable = true;
                item.dataset.name = file.name;
                item.dataset.type = file.type;
                item.dataset.index = index;
                
                const icon = getFileIcon(file.name, file.type);
                const size = file.type === 'directory' ? '--' : formatSize(file.size);
                
                item.innerHTML = `
                    <i class="${icon} text-lg ${file.type === 'directory' ? 'text-yellow-500' : 'text-blue-400'} w-6 text-center"></i>
                    <div class="flex-1 min-w-0">
                        <div class="text-sm font-medium truncate">${file.name}</div>
                        <div class="text-xs text-gray-500">${size} • ${file.modified || 'Unknown'}</div>
                    </div>
                `;
                
                // Events
                item.addEventListener('click', (e) => selectFile(panel, index, e));
                item.addEventListener('dblclick', () => openFile(panel, file));
                item.addEventListener('contextmenu', (e) => showContextMenu(e, panel, file));
                
                // Drag events
                item.addEventListener('dragstart', (e) => handleDragStart(e, panel, file));
                item.addEventListener('dragend', (e) => handleDragEnd(e));
                
                container.appendChild(item);
            });
        }

        // UI Helpers
        function getFileIcon(name, type) {
            if (type === 'directory') return 'fas fa-folder';
            
            const ext = name.split('.').pop().toLowerCase();
            const iconMap = {
                'js': 'fab fa-js text-yellow-400',
                'html': 'fab fa-html5 text-orange-500',
                'css': 'fab fa-css3 text-blue-500',
                'json': 'fas fa-code text-gray-400',
                'md': 'fas fa-markdown text-white',
                'txt': 'fas fa-file-alt text-gray-400',
                'py': 'fab fa-python text-blue-300',
                'jpg': 'fas fa-image text-purple-400',
                'png': 'fas fa-image text-purple-400'
            };
            return iconMap[ext] || 'fas fa-file text-gray-400';
        }

        function formatSize(bytes) {
            if (bytes === 0) return '0 B';
            const k = 1024;
            const sizes = ['B', 'KB', 'MB', 'GB'];
            const i = Math.floor(Math.log(bytes) / Math.log(k));
            return parseFloat((bytes / Math.pow(k, i)).toFixed(1)) + ' ' + sizes[i];
        }

        function updateBreadcrumb(panel, path) {
            const container = document.getElementById(`${panel}-breadcrumb`);
            container.innerHTML = '';
            
            const parts = path.split('/').filter(p => p);
            let currentPath = '';
            
            // Root
            const root = document.createElement('span');
            root.className = 'breadcrumb-item cursor-pointer hover:text-blue-400';
            root.textContent = panel === 'local' ? '/' : 'root';
            root.onclick = () => navigateTo(panel, '');
            container.appendChild(root);
            
            parts.forEach((part, i) => {
                const separator = document.createElement('span');
                separator.className = 'text-gray-600';
                separator.textContent = ' / ';
                container.appendChild(separator);
                
                currentPath += (panel === 'local' ? '/' : '') + part;
                const span = document.createElement('span');
                span.className = 'breadcrumb-item cursor-pointer hover:text-blue-400';
                span.textContent = part;
                const pathSnapshot = currentPath;
                span.onclick = () => navigateTo(panel, pathSnapshot);
                container.appendChild(span);
            });
        }

        // Navigation
        function navigateTo(panel, path) {
            if (panel === 'local') {
                loadLocalFiles(path || '/storage/emulated/0');
            } else {
                loadGitHubFiles(path);
            }
        }

        function navigateUp(panel) {
            const current = panel === 'local' ? state.local.currentPath : state.github.currentPath;
            if (!current || current === '/storage/emulated/0') return;
            
            const parent = current.split('/').slice(0, -1).join('/') || '/storage/emulated/0';
            navigateTo(panel, parent);
        }

        function refreshPanel(panel) {
            if (panel === 'local') {
                loadLocalFiles(state.local.currentPath);
            } else {
                loadGitHubFiles(state.github.currentPath);
            }
        }

        // File Selection & Opening
        function selectFile(panel, index, event) {
            const container = document.getElementById(`${panel}-files`);
            const items = container.querySelectorAll('.file-item');
            
            if (!event.ctrlKey && !event.shiftKey) {
                items.forEach(i => i.classList.remove('selected'));
            }
            
            items[index].classList.add('selected');
            
            if (panel === 'local') {
                state.local.selected = state.local.files[index];
            } else {
                state.github.selected = state.github.files[index];
            }
        }

        async function openFile(panel, file) {
            if (file.type === 'directory') {
                const newPath = panel === 'local' 
                    ? `${state.local.currentPath}/${file.name}`
                    : `${state.github.currentPath}/${file.name}`.replace(/^\/+/, '');
                navigateTo(panel, newPath);
                return;
            }
            
            // Open in editor
            openEditor(panel, file);
        }

        // Editor Operations
        async function openEditor(panel, file) {
            state.editor.currentFile = { panel, file };
            state.editor.visible = true;
            
            document.getElementById('editor-filename').textContent = file.name;
            document.getElementById('editor-filename').classList.remove('text-yellow-400');
            
            // Show editor panel
            const editorPanel = document.getElementById('editor-panel');
            const resizer2 = document.getElementById('resizer-2');
            editorPanel.style.width = '600px';
            resizer2.classList.remove('hidden');
            
            // Load content
            let content = '';
            if (panel === 'local') {
                // Fetch from local API
                content = await fetchLocalFile(file.name);
            } else {
                // Fetch from GitHub
                content = await fetchGitHubFile(file.path || file.name);
            }
            
            // Set Monaco content
            if (state.editorInstance) {
                const lang = getLanguage(file.name);
                state.monaco.editor.setModelLanguage(state.editorInstance.getModel(), lang);
                state.editorInstance.setValue(content);
                state.editor.modified = false;
                document.getElementById('editor-lang').textContent = lang;
            }
        }

        function closeEditor() {
            if (state.editor.modified && !confirm('Discard changes?')) return;
            
            state.editor.visible = false;
            state.editor.currentFile = null;
            
            const editorPanel = document.getElementById('editor-panel');
            const resizer2 = document.getElementById('resizer-2');
            editorPanel.style.width = '0';
            resizer2.classList.add('hidden');
        }

        function toggleEditor() {
            if (state.editor.visible) {
                closeEditor();
            } else if (state.editor.currentFile) {
                openEditor(state.editor.currentFile.panel, state.editor.currentFile.file);
            }
        }

        async function saveCurrentFile() {
            if (!state.editor.currentFile) return;
            
            const { panel, file } = state.editor.currentFile;
            const content = state.editorInstance.getValue();
            
            showNotification('Saving...', 'info');
            
            try {
                if (panel === 'local') {
                    await saveLocalFile(file.name, content);
                } else {
                    await saveGitHubFile(file.path || file.name, content, file.sha);
                }
                
                state.editor.modified = false;
                document.getElementById('editor-filename').classList.remove('text-yellow-400');
                showNotification('Saved successfully', 'success');
            } catch (err) {
                showNotification('Save failed: ' + err.message, 'error');
            }
        }

        function getLanguage(filename) {
            const ext = filename.split('.').pop().toLowerCase();
            const langMap = {
                'js': 'javascript',
                'ts': 'typescript',
                'html': 'html',
                'css': 'css',
                'json': 'json',
                'md': 'markdown',
                'py': 'python',
                'java': 'java',
                'cpp': 'cpp',
                'c': 'c',
                'go': 'go',
                'rs': 'rust'
            };
            return langMap[ext] || 'plaintext';
        }

        // Drag and Drop
        function handleDragStart(e, panel, file) {
            e.target.classList.add('dragging');
            e.dataTransfer.effectAllowed = 'copyMove';
            e.dataTransfer.setData('application/json', JSON.stringify({ panel, file }));
        }

        function handleDragEnd(e) {
            e.target.classList.remove('dragging');
        }

        function setupDragAndDrop() {
            const panels = ['local-files', 'github-files'];
            
            panels.forEach(id => {
                const container = document.getElementById(id);
                const targetPanel = id === 'local-files' ? 'local' : 'github';
                
                container.addEventListener('dragover', (e) => {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    e.dataTransfer.dropEffect = 'copy';
                });
                
                container.addEventListener('dragenter', (e) => {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    container.classList.add('drag-over');
                });
                
                container.addEventListener('dragleave', (e) => {
                    container.classList.remove('drag-over');
                });
                
                container.addEventListener('drop', async (e) => {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    container.classList.remove('drag-over');
                    
                    const data = e.dataTransfer.getData('application/json');
                    if (!data) return;
                    
                    const { panel: sourcePanel, file } = JSON.parse(data);
                    if (sourcePanel === targetPanel) return; // Same panel
                    
                    await transferFile(sourcePanel, targetPanel, file);
                });
            });
        }

        async function transferFile(from, to, file) {
            if (file.type === 'directory') {
                showNotification('Directory transfer not yet implemented', 'warning');
                return;
            }
            
            showTransferProgress(true, `Transferring ${file.name}...`);
            
            try {
                if (from === 'local' && to === 'github') {
                    // Local to GitHub
                    const content = await fetchLocalFile(file.name);
                    const path = `${state.github.currentPath}/${file.name}`.replace(/^\/+/, '');
                    await createGitHubFile(path, content);
                } else {
                    // GitHub to Local
                    const content = await fetchGitHubFile(file.path || file.name);
                    await saveLocalFile(file.name, content, state.local.currentPath);
                }
                
                showTransferProgress(false);
                showNotification('Transfer complete', 'success');
                refreshPanel(to);
            } catch (err) {
                showTransferProgress(false);
                showNotification('Transfer failed: ' + err.message, 'error');
            }
        }

        // Context Menu
        function showContextMenu(e, panel, file) {
            e.preventDefault();
            const menu = document.getElementById('context-menu');
            const header = document.getElementById('ctx-header');
            
            menu.style.left = `${e.clientX}px`;
            menu.style.top = `${e.clientY}px`;
            menu.classList.remove('hidden');
            
            header.textContent = file.name;
            state.contextMenuTarget = { panel, file };
            
            // Hide on click elsewhere
            setTimeout(() => {
                document.addEventListener('click', hideContextMenu, { once: true });
            }, 0);
        }

        function hideContextMenu() {
            document.getElementById('context-menu').classList.add('hidden');
        }

        function ctxAction(action) {
            const { panel, file } = state.contextMenuTarget;
            hideContextMenu();
            
            switch(action) {
                case 'open':
                    openFile(panel, file);
                    break;
                case 'copy':
                    copyToClipboard(panel, file);
                    break;
                case 'cut':
                    cutToClipboard(panel, file);
                    break;
                case 'paste':
                    pasteFromClipboard(panel);
                    break;
                case 'rename':
                    renameFile(panel, file);
                    break;
                case 'delete':
                    deleteFile(panel, file);
                    break;
                case 'transfer':
                    const target = panel === 'local' ? 'github' : 'local';
                    transferFile(panel, target, file);
                    break;
            }
        }

        // Clipboard Operations
        function copyToClipboard(panel, file) {
            if (panel === 'local') {
                state.local.clipboard = file;
                state.local.clipboardAction = 'copy';
            } else {
                state.github.clipboard = file;
                state.github.clipboardAction = 'copy';
            }
            showNotification('Copied to clipboard', 'info');
        }

        function cutToClipboard(panel, file) {
            if (panel === 'local') {
                state.local.clipboard = file;
                state.local.clipboardAction = 'cut';
            } else {
                state.github.clipboard = file;
                state.github.clipboardAction = 'cut';
            }
            showNotification('Cut to clipboard', 'info');
        }

        async function pasteFromClipboard(panel) {
            const clipboard = panel === 'local' ? state.local.clipboard : state.github.clipboard;
            const action = panel === 'local' ? state.local.clipboardAction : state.github.clipboardAction;
            
            if (!clipboard) {
                showNotification('Clipboard empty', 'warning');
                return;
            }
            
            // Implement paste logic here
            showNotification('Pasting...', 'info');
        }

        // File Operations
        async function deleteFile(panel, file) {
            if (!confirm(`Delete ${file.name}?`)) return;
            
            try {
                if (panel === 'local') {
                    await deleteLocalFile(file.name);
                } else {
                    await deleteGitHubFile(file.path || file.name, file.sha);
                }
                showNotification('Deleted', 'success');
                refreshPanel(panel);
            } catch (err) {
                showNotification('Delete failed: ' + err.message, 'error');
            }
        }

        function renameFile(panel, file) {
            const newName = prompt('New name:', file.name);
            if (!newName || newName === file.name) return;
            
            // Implement rename
        }

        // GitHub Config
        function showGitHubConfig() {
            const config = document.getElementById('github-config');
            config.classList.toggle('hidden');
        }

        function connectGitHub() {
            const token = document.getElementById('gh-token').value;
            const repo = document.getElementById('gh-repo').value;
            
            if (!token || !repo) {
                showNotification('Please enter both token and repo', 'error');
                return;
            }
            
            state.github.token = token;
            state.github.repo = repo;
            localStorage.setItem('gh_token', token);
            localStorage.setItem('gh_repo', repo);
            
            document.getElementById('github-config').classList.add('hidden');
            loadGitHubFiles('');
            showNotification('Connected to GitHub', 'success');
        }

        // Resizing
        function setupResizers() {
            const resizer1 = document.getElementById('resizer-1');
            const resizer2 = document.getElementById('resizer-2');
            const leftPanel = document.getElementById('left-panel');
            const editorPanel = document.getElementById('editor-panel');
            const rightPanel = document.getElementById('right-panel');
            
            let isResizing = false;
            let currentResizer = null;
            
            function initResize(e, resizer) {
                isResizing = true;
                currentResizer = resizer;
                resizer.classList.add('active');
                document.body.style.cursor = 'col-resize';
                e.preventDefault();
            }
            
            resizer1.addEventListener('mousedown', (e) => initResize(e, resizer1));
            resizer2.addEventListener('mousedown', (e) => initResize(e, resizer2));
            
            document.addEventListener('mousemove', (e) => {
                if (!isResizing) return;
                
                if (currentResizer === resizer1) {
                    const newWidth = e.clientX;
                    if (newWidth > 200 && newWidth < window.innerWidth * 0.5) {
                        leftPanel.style.flex = 'none';
                        leftPanel.style.width = `${newWidth}px`;
                    }
                } else if (currentResizer === resizer2 && state.editor.visible) {
                    const containerRect = document.querySelector('.flex-1.flex').getBoundingClientRect();
                    const relativeX = e.clientX - containerRect.left;
                    const editorWidth = relativeX - leftPanel.offsetWidth - resizer1.offsetWidth;
                    
                    if (editorWidth > 300 && editorWidth < 800) {
                        editorPanel.style.width = `${editorWidth}px`;
                    }
                }
            });
            
            document.addEventListener('mouseup', () => {
                isResizing = false;
                if (currentResizer) {
                    currentResizer.classList.remove('active');
                    currentResizer = null;
                }
                document.body.style.cursor = '';
            });
        }

        // Keyboard Shortcuts
        function setupKeyboardShortcuts() {
            document.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
                if (e.ctrlKey || e.metaKey) {
                    switch(e.key) {
                        case 's':
                            e.preventDefault();
                            if (state.editor.visible) saveCurrentFile();
                            break;
                        case 'c':
                            // Copy selected file
                            break;
                        case 'v':
                            // Paste
                            break;
                    }
                }
                
                if (e.key === 'F5') {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    refreshPanel('local');
                    refreshPanel('github');
                }
                
                if (e.key === 'Escape') {
                    closeEditor();
                    hideContextMenu();
                }
            });
        }

        // API Implementations (Mock - Replace with actual backend calls)
        async function fetchLocalFile(filename) {
            // Replace with: return fetch(`/api/local/read?path=${encodeURIComponent(path)}`).then(r => r.text())
            return `// Content of ${filename}\n// Replace with actual API call\n\nconsole.log("Hello from local file");`;
        }

        async function saveLocalFile(filename, content, path) {
            // Replace with: return fetch('/api/local/write', {method: 'POST', body: JSON.stringify({path, content})})
            console.log('Saving local:', filename);
            return new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 500));
        }

        async function deleteLocalFile(filename) {
            // Replace with actual API
            return new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 500));
        }

        async function fetchGitHubFile(path) {
            const response = await fetch(`https://api.github.com/repos/${state.github.repo}/contents/${path}?ref=${state.github.branch}`, {
                headers: { 'Authorization': `token ${state.github.token}` }
            });
            const data = await response.json();
            return atob(data.content);
        }

        async function saveGitHubFile(path, content, sha) {
            const message = `Update ${path} via MT-Git Manager`;
            const content_encoded = btoa(content);
            
            const body = {
                message,
                content: content_encoded,
                sha: sha,
                branch: state.github.branch
            };
            
            const response = await fetch(`https://api.github.com/repos/${state.github.repo}/contents/${path}`, {
                method: 'PUT',
                headers: {
                    'Authorization': `token ${state.github.token}`,
                    'Content-Type': 'application/json'
                },
                body: JSON.stringify(body)
            });
            
            if (!response.ok) throw new Error('Failed to save');
            return response.json();
        }

        async function createGitHubFile(path, content) {
            const message = `Create ${path} via MT-Git Manager`;
            const content_encoded = btoa(content);
            
            const response = await fetch(`https://api.github.com/repos/${state.github.repo}/contents/${path}`, {
                method: 'PUT',
                headers: {
                    'Authorization': `token ${state.github.token}`,
                    'Content-Type': 'application/json'
                },
                body: JSON.stringify({
                    message,
                    content: content_encoded,
                    branch: state.github.branch
                })
            });
            
            if (!response.ok) throw new Error('Failed to create');
        }

        async function deleteGitHubFile(path, sha) {
            const response = await fetch(`https://api.github.com/repos/${state.github.repo}/contents/${path}`, {
                method: 'DELETE',
                headers: {
                    'Authorization': `token ${state.github.token}`,
                    'Content-Type': 'application/json'
                },
                body: JSON.stringify({
                    message: `Delete ${path} via MT-Git Manager`,
                    sha: sha,
                    branch: state.github.branch
                })
            });
            
            if (!response.ok) throw new Error('Failed to delete');
        }

        // Utilities
        function generateMockFiles(path) {
            // Generate random mock files for demo
            return Array.from({length: 5}, (_, i) => ({
                name: `file_${i}.txt`,
                type: 'file',
                size: Math.floor(Math.random() * 10000),
                modified: '2024-01-01'
            }));
        }

        function showLoading(panel, show) {
            const container = document.getElementById(`${panel}-files`);
            if (show) {
                container.style.opacity = '0.5';
            } else {
                container.style.opacity = '1';
            }
        }

        function showTransferProgress(show, text) {
            const modal = document.getElementById('transfer-modal');
            const textEl = document.getElementById('transfer-text');
            
            if (show) {
                modal.classList.remove('hidden');
                modal.classList.add('flex');
                textEl.textContent = text;
                document.getElementById('transfer-progress').style.width = '0%';
                
                // Simulate progress
                setTimeout(() => {
                    document.getElementById('transfer-progress').style.width = '50%';
                }, 100);
            } else {
                document.getElementById('transfer-progress').style.width = '100%';
                setTimeout(() => {
                    modal.classList.add('hidden');
                    modal.classList.remove('flex');
                }, 300);
            }
        }

        function showNotification(message, type = 'info') {
            // Simple notification implementation
            const div = document.createElement('div');
            const colors = {
                success: 'bg-green-600',
                error: 'bg-red-600',
                warning: 'bg-yellow-600',
                info: 'bg-blue-600'
            };
            
            div.className = `fixed bottom-4 right-4 ${colors[type]} text-white px-4 py-2 rounded shadow-lg z-50 animate-fade-in`;
            div.textContent = message;
            document.body.appendChild(div);
            
            setTimeout(() => {
                div.remove();
            }, 3000);
        }

        // Toggle editor button
        document.getElementById('toggle-editor').addEventListener('click', toggleEditor);
    </script>
</body>
</html>

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
// server/routes/github.js
const express = require('express');
const router = express.Router();
const githubService = require('../services/githubService');

// POST /api/github/connect
router.post('/connect', async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const { token, repo } = req.body;
        
        if (!token || !repo) {
            return res.status(400).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'Token and repo (owner/name) required'
            });
        }

        // Validate connection by fetching repo info
        const repoInfo = await githubService.validateConnection(token, repo);
        
        // Store credentials in service (memory only)
        githubService.setCredentials(token, repo);
        
        res.json({
            success: true,
            message: 'Connected to GitHub successfully',
            repo: repoInfo
        });
    } catch (error) {
        res.status(401).json({
            success: false,
            error: error.message
        });
    }
});

// GET /api/github/list?path=
router.get('/list', async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const { path = '' } = req.query;
        
        if (!githubService.isConnected()) {
            return res.status(401).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'Not connected to GitHub. Call /connect first.'
            });
        }

        const files = await githubService.listContents(path);
        
        res.json({
            success: true,
            path: path,
            files: files
        });
    } catch (error) {
        res.status(500).json({
            success: false,
            error: error.message
        });
    }
});

// GET /api/github/read?path=
router.get('/read', async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const { path } = req.query;
        
        if (!path) {
            return res.status(400).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'Path parameter required'
            });
        }

        if (!githubService.isConnected()) {
            return res.status(401).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'Not connected to GitHub'
            });
        }

        const content = await githubService.getFileContent(path);
        
        res.json({
            success: true,
            path: path,
            content: content,
            encoding: 'utf-8'
        });
    } catch (error) {
        res.status(500).json({
            success: false,
            error: error.message
        });
    }
});

// POST /api/github/create
router.post('/create', async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const { path: filePath, content, message = `Create ${filePath} via MT-Git Manager` } = req.body;
        
        if (!filePath || content === undefined) {
            return res.status(400).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'Path and content required'
            });
        }

        if (!githubService.isConnected()) {
            return res.status(401).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'Not connected to GitHub'
            });
        }

        const result = await githubService.createFile(filePath, content, message);
        
        res.json({
            success: true,
            message: 'File created successfully',
            commit: result.commit,
            content: result.content
        });
    } catch (error) {
        res.status(500).json({
            success: false,
            error: error.message
        });
    }
});

// POST /api/github/update
router.post('/update', async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const { path: filePath, content, sha, message = `Update ${filePath} via MT-Git Manager` } = req.body;
        
        if (!filePath || content === undefined || !sha) {
            return res.status(400).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'Path, content, and sha required'
            });
        }

        if (!githubService.isConnected()) {
            return res.status(401).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'Not connected to GitHub'
            });
        }

        const result = await githubService.updateFile(filePath, content, sha, message);
        
        res.json({
            success: true,
            message: 'File updated successfully',
            commit: result.commit,
            content: result.content
        });
    } catch (error) {
        res.status(500).json({
            success: false,
            error: error.message
        });
    }
});

// POST /api/github/delete
router.post('/delete', async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const { path: filePath, sha, message = `Delete ${filePath} via MT-Git Manager` } = req.body;
        
        if (!filePath || !sha) {
            return res.status(400).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'Path and sha required'
            });
        }

        if (!githubService.isConnected()) {
            return res.status(401).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'Not connected to GitHub'
            });
        }

        const result = await githubService.deleteFile(filePath, sha, message);
        
        res.json({
            success: true,
            message: 'File deleted successfully',
            commit: result.commit
        });
    } catch (error) {
        res.status(500).json({
            success: false,
            error: error.message
        });
    }
});

// GET /api/github/branches
router.get('/branches', async (req, res) => {
    try {
        if (!githubService.isConnected()) {
            return res.status(401).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'Not connected to GitHub'
            });
        }

        const branches = await githubService.listBranches();
        
        res.json({
            success: true,
            branches: branches
        });
    } catch (error) {
        res.status(500).json({
            success: false,
            error: error.message
        });
    }
});

module.exports = router;

```javascript
// server/routes/localStorage.js
const express = require('express');
const router = express.Router();
const filesystemService = require('../services/filesystemService');

// GET /api/local/list?path=/storage/emulated/0/Documents
router.get('/list', async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const { path: dirPath } = req.query;
        
        if (!dirPath) {
```

```javascript

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/gitm/server/routes/transfer.js
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
// server/routes/transfer.js
const express = require('express');
const router = express.Router();
const filesystemService = require('../services/filesystemService');
const githubService = require('../services/githubService');

// POST /api/transfer/local-to-github
router.post('/local-to-github', async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const { localPath, githubPath, message } = req.body;
        
        if (!localPath || !githubPath) {
            return res.status(400).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'Both localPath and githubPath required'
            });
        }

        if (!githubService.isConnected()) {
            return res.status(401).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'GitHub not connected'
            });
        }

        // Step 1: Read local file
        console.log(`[Transfer] Reading local file: ${localPath}`);
        const content = await filesystemService.readFile(localPath);
        
        // Step 2: Check if file exists on GitHub (for update vs create)
        let sha = null;
        try {
            const existingFile = await githubService.getFileInfo(githubPath);
            sha = existingFile.sha;
        } catch (err) {
            // File doesn't exist, will create new
        }

        // Step 3: Transfer to GitHub
        console.log(`[Transfer] Writing to GitHub: ${githubPath}`);
        let result;
        const commitMessage = message || `Transfer ${localPath.split('/').pop()} via MT-Git Manager`;
        
        if (sha) {
            // Update existing
            result = await githubService.updateFile(githubPath, content, sha, commitMessage);
        } else {
            // Create new
            result = await githubService.createFile(githubPath, content, commitMessage);
        }

        res.json({
            success: true,
            message: 'Transfer completed successfully',
            source: localPath,
            destination: githubPath,
            commit: result.commit
        });
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('[Transfer Error]', error);
        res.status(500).json({
            success: false,
            error: error.message,
            stage: error.stage || 'unknown'
        });
    }
});

// POST /api/transfer/github-to-local
router.post('/github-to-local', async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const { githubPath, localPath } = req.body;
        
        if (!githubPath || !localPath) {
            return res.status(400).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'Both githubPath and localPath required'
            });
        }

        if (!githubService.isConnected()) {
            return res.status(401).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'GitHub not connected'
            });
        }

        // Step 1: Fetch from GitHub
        console.log(`[Transfer] Fetching from GitHub: ${githubPath}`);
        const content = await githubService.getFileContent(githubPath);
        
        // Step 2: Write to local storage
        console.log(`[Transfer] Writing to local: ${localPath}`);
        await filesystemService.writeFile(localPath, content);

        res.json({
            success: true,
            message: 'Transfer completed successfully',
            source: githubPath,
            destination: localPath
        });
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('[Transfer Error]', error);
        res.status(500).json({
            success: false,
            error: error.message,
            stage: error.stage || 'unknown'
        });
    }
});

// POST /api/transfer/batch
router.post('/batch', async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const { operations } = req.body;
        
        if (!Array.isArray(operations)) {
            return res.status(400).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'Operations array required'
            });
        }

        const results = [];
        const errors = [];

        for (const op of operations) {
            try {
                if (op.direction === 'local-to-github') {
                    const content = await filesystemService.readFile(op.source);
                    let sha = null;
                    try {
                        const info = await githubService.getFileInfo(op.destination);
                        sha = info.sha;
                    } catch (e) {}
                    
                    if (sha) {
                        await githubService.updateFile(op.destination, content, sha, op.message);
                    } else {
                        await githubService.createFile(op.destination, content, op.message);
                    }
                } else {
                    const content = await githubService.getFileContent(op.source);
                    await filesystemService.writeFile(op.destination, content);
                }
                results.push({ success: true, operation: op });
            } catch (err) {
                errors.push({ success: false, operation: op, error: err.message });
            }
        }

        res.json({
            success: errors.length === 0,
            completed: results.length,
            failed: errors.length,
            results,
            errors
        });
    } catch (error) {
        res.status(500).json({
            success: false,
            error: error.message
        });
    }
});

module.exports = router;
```

```javascriptconst express = require('express');

const filesystemService = require('../services/filesystemService');
const githubService = require('../services/githubService');

// POST /api/transfer/local-to-github
router.post('/local-to-github', async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const { localPath, githubPath, message } = req.body;
        
        if (!localPath || !githubPath) {
            return res.status(400).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'Both localPath and githubPath required'
            });
        }

        if (!githubService.isConnected()) {
            return res.status(401).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'GitHub not connected'
            });
        }

        // Step 1: Read local file
        console.log(`[Transfer] Reading local file: ${localPath}`);
        const content = await filesystemService.readFile(localPath);
        
        // Step 2: Check if file exists on GitHub (for update vs create)
        let sha = null;
        try {
            const existingFile = await githubService.getFileInfo(githubPath);
            sha = existingFile.sha;
        } catch (err) {
            // File doesn't exist, will create new
        }

        // Step 3: Transfer to GitHub
        console.log(`[Transfer] Writing to GitHub: ${githubPath}`);
        let result;
        const commitMessage = message || `Transfer ${localPath.split('/').pop()} via MT-Git Manager`;
        
        if (sha) {
            // Update existing
            result = await githubService.updateFile(githubPath, content, sha, commitMessage);
        } else {
            // Create new
            result = await githubService.createFile(githubPath, content, commitMessage);
        }

        res.json({
            success: true,
            message: 'Transfer completed successfully',
            source: localPath,
            destination: githubPath,
            commit: result.commit
        });
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('[Transfer Error]', error);
        res.status(500).json({
            success: false,
            error: error.message,
            stage: error.stage || 'unknown'
        });
    }
});

// POST /api/transfer/github-to-local
router.post('/github-to-local', async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const { githubPath, localPath } = req.body;
        
        if (!githubPath || !localPath) {
            return res.status(400).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'Both githubPath and localPath required'
            });
        }

        if (!githubService.isConnected()) {
            return res.status(401).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'GitHub not connected'
            });
        }

        // Step 1: Fetch from GitHub
        console.log(`[Transfer] Fetching from GitHub: ${githubPath}`);
        const content = await githubService.getFileContent(githubPath);
        
        // Step 2: Write to local storage
        console.log(`[Transfer] Writing to local: ${localPath}`);
        await filesystemService.writeFile(localPath, content);

        res.json({
            success: true,
            message: 'Transfer completed successfully',
            source: githubPath,
            destination: localPath
        });
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('[Transfer Error]', error);
        res.status(500).json({
            success: false,
            error: error.message,
            stage: error.stage || 'unknown'
        });
    }
});

// POST /api/transfer/batch
router.post('/batch', async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const { operations } = req.body;
        
        if (!Array.isArray(operations)) {
            return res.status(400).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'Operations array required'
            });
        }

        const results = [];
        const errors = [];

        for (const op of operations) {
            try {
                if (op.direction === 'local-to-github') {
                    const content = await filesystemService.readFile(op.source);
                    let sha = null;
                    try {
                        const info = await githubService.getFileInfo(op.destination);
                        sha = info.sha;
                    } catch (e) {}
                    
                    if (sha) {
                        await githubService.updateFile(op.destination, content, sha, op.message);
                    } else {
                        await githubService.createFile(op.destination, content, op.message);
                    }
                } else {
                    const content = await githubService.getFileContent(op.source);
                    await filesystemService.writeFile(op.destination, content);
                }
                results.push({ success: true, operation: op });
            } catch (err) {
                errors.push({ success: false, operation: op, error: err.message });
            }
        }

        res.json({
            success: errors.length === 0,
            completed: results.length,
            failed: errors.length,
            results,
            errors
        });
    } catch (error) {
        res.status(500).json({
            success: false,
            error: error.message
        });
    }
});

module.exports = router;
```

```javascript
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/gitm/server/services/filesystemService.js
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
// server/services/filesystemService.js
const fs = require('fs').promises;
const path = require('path');
const pathUtils = require('../utils/pathUtils');

const BASE_PATH = '/';

class FilesystemService {
    constructor() {
        this.basePath = BASE_PATH;
    }

    // Ensure path is valid (removed sandbox restriction)
    sanitizePath(inputPath) {
        // Normalize path
        let normalized = path.normalize(inputPath);

        // Resolve absolute path
        normalized = path.resolve(normalized);

        // If relative path, join with current working directory
        if (!normalized.startsWith('/')) {
            normalized = path.join(process.cwd(), normalized);
        }

        return normalized;
    }

    async listDirectory(dirPath) {
        const safePath = this.sanitizePath(dirPath);

        try {
            const entries = await fs.readdir(safePath, { withFileTypes: true });

            const files = await Promise.all(entries.map(async (entry) => {
                const fullPath = path.join(safePath, entry.name);
                const stats = await fs.stat(fullPath).catch(() => null);

                return {
                    name: entry.name,
                    type: entry.isDirectory() ? 'directory' : 'file',
                    size: stats ? stats.size : 0,
                    modified: stats ? stats.mtime.toISOString() : new Date().toISOString(),
                    permissions: stats ? stats.mode.toString(8) : 'unknown'
                };
            }));

            // Sort: directories first, then alphabetically
            return files.sort((a, b) => {
                if (a.type === b.type) return a.name.localeCompare(b.name);
                return a.type === 'directory' ? -1 : 1;
            });
        } catch (error) {
            throw new Error(`Cannot read directory: ${error.message}`);
        }
    }

    async readFile(filePath) {
        const safePath = this.sanitizePath(filePath);

        try {
            // Check if file is binary (images, etc.)
            const ext = path.extname(safePath).toLowerCase();
            const binaryExts = ['.png', '.jpg', '.jpeg', '.gif', '.ico', '.pdf', '.zip', '.mp4', '.mp3', '.webm'];

            if (binaryExts.includes(ext)) {
                return await fs.readFile(safePath);
            }

            return await fs.readFile(safePath, 'utf-8');
        } catch (error) {
            throw new Error(`Cannot read file: ${error.message}`);
        }
    }

    async writeFile(filePath, content) {
        const safePath = this.sanitizePath(filePath);

        try {
            // Ensure directory exists
            const dir = path.dirname(safePath);
            await fs.mkdir(dir, { recursive: true });

            await fs.writeFile(safePath, content, 'utf-8');
            return true;
        } catch (error) {
            throw new Error(`Cannot write file: ${error.message}`);
        }
    }

    async deleteFile(filePath) {
        const safePath = this.sanitizePath(filePath);

        try {
            const stats = await fs.stat(safePath);

            if (stats.isDirectory()) {
                await fs.rmdir(safePath, { recursive: true });
            } else {
                await fs.unlink(safePath);
            }

            return true;
        } catch (error) {
            throw new Error(`Cannot delete: ${error.message}`);
        }
    }

    async renameFile(oldPath, newPath) {
        const safeOld = this.sanitizePath(oldPath);
        const safeNew = this.sanitizePath(newPath);

        try {
            await fs.rename(safeOld, safeNew);
            return true;
        } catch (error) {
            throw new Error(`Cannot rename: ${error.message}`);
        }
    }

    async createDirectory(dirPath) {
        const safePath = this.sanitizePath(dirPath);

        try {
            await fs.mkdir(safePath, { recursive: true });
            return true;
        } catch (error) {
            throw new Error(`Cannot create directory: ${error.message}`);
        }
    }

    async fileExists(filePath) {
        try {
            const safePath = this.sanitizePath(filePath);
            await fs.access(safePath);
            return true;
        } catch {
            return false;
        }
    }

    async getFileStats(filePath) {
        const safePath = this.sanitizePath(filePath);
        return await fs.stat(safePath);
    }

    // New: Get available storage locations
    async getSystemRoots() {
        return [
            { path: '/', name: 'Root Filesystem' },
            { path: '/storage/emulated/0', name: 'Internal Storage' },
            { path: '/data/data/com.termux/files/home', name: 'Termux Home' },
            { path: '/sdcard', name: 'SD Card' },
            { path: '/system', name: 'System (Read-only)' },
            { path: '/vendor', name: 'Vendor (Read-only)' },
            { path: process.cwd(), name: 'Current Working Directory' }
        ];
    }
}

module.exports = new FilesystemService();

const fs = require('fs').promises;
const path = require('path');
const pathUtils = require('../utils/pathUtils');

const BASE_PATH = '/storage/emulated/0';

class FilesystemService {
    constructor() {
        this.basePath = BASE_PATH;
    }

    // Ensure path is within allowed directory
    sanitizePath(inputPath) {
        // Normalize path
        let normalized = path.normalize(inputPath);
        
        // Remove any .. sequences
        if (normalized.includes('..')) {
            throw new Error('Invalid path: directory traversal detected');
        }
        
        // Ensure path starts with base path
        if (!normalized.startsWith(this.basePath)) {
            // If relative path provided, join with base
            if (!normalized.startsWith('/')) {
                normalized = path.join(this.basePath, normalized);
            } else {
                throw new Error('Invalid path: outside allowed directory');
            }
        }
        
        return normalized;
    }

    async listDirectory(dirPath) {
        const safePath = this.sanitizePath(dirPath);
        
        try {
            const entries = await fs.readdir(safePath, { withFileTypes: true });
            
            const files = await Promise.all(entries.map(async (entry) => {
                const fullPath = path.join(safePath, entry.name);
                const stats = await fs.stat(fullPath).catch(() => null);
                
                return {
                    name: entry.name,
                    type: entry.isDirectory() ? 'directory' : 'file',
                    size: stats ? stats.size : 0,
                    modified: stats ? stats.mtime.toISOString() : new Date().toISOString(),
                    permissions: stats ? stats.mode.toString(8) : 'unknown'
                };
            }));
            
            // Sort: directories first, then alphabetically
            return files.sort((a, b) => {
                if (a.type === b.type) return a.name.localeCompare(b.name);
                return a.type === 'directory' ? -1 : 1;
            });
        } catch (error) {
            throw new Error(`Cannot read directory: ${error.message}`);
        }
    }

    async readFile(filePath) {
        const safePath = this.sanitizePath(filePath);
        
        try {
            // Check if file is binary (images, etc.)
            const ext = path.extname(safePath).toLowerCase();
            const binaryExts = ['.png', '.jpg', '.jpeg', '.gif', '.ico', '.pdf', '.zip'];
            
            if (binaryExts.includes(ext)) {
                return await fs.readFile(safePath);
            }
            
            return await fs.readFile(safePath, 'utf-8');
        } catch (error) {
            throw new Error(`Cannot read file: ${error.message}`);
        }
    }

    async writeFile(filePath, content) {
        const safePath = this.sanitizePath(filePath);
        
        try {
            // Ensure directory exists
            const dir = path.dirname(safePath);
            await fs.mkdir(dir, { recursive: true });
            
            await fs.writeFile(safePath, content, 'utf-8');
            return true;
        } catch (error) {
            throw new Error(`Cannot write file: ${error.message}`);
        }
    }

    async deleteFile(filePath) {
        const safePath = this.sanitizePath(filePath);
        
        try {
            const stats = await fs.stat(safePath);
            
            if (stats.isDirectory()) {
                await fs.rmdir(safePath, { recursive: true });
            } else {
                await fs.unlink(safePath);
            }
            
            return true;
        } catch (error) {
            throw new Error(`Cannot delete: ${error.message}`);
        }
    }

    async renameFile(oldPath, newPath) {
        const safeOld = this.sanitizePath(oldPath);
        const safeNew = this.sanitizePath(newPath);
        
        try {
            await fs.rename(safeOld, safeNew);
            return true;
        } catch (error) {
            throw new Error(`Cannot rename: ${error.message}`);
        }
    }

    async createDirectory(dirPath) {
        const safePath = this.sanitizePath(dirPath);
        
        try {
            await fs.mkdir(safePath, { recursive: true });
            return true;
        } catch (error) {
            throw new Error(`Cannot create directory: ${error.message}`);
        }
    }

    async fileExists(filePath) {
        try {
            const safePath = this.sanitizePath(filePath);
            await fs.access(safePath);
            return true;
        } catch {
            return false;
        }
    }

    async getFileStats(filePath) {
        const safePath = this.sanitizePath(filePath);
        return await fs.stat(safePath);
    }
}

module.exports = new FilesystemService();
```

```javascript
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/gitm/server/services/githubService.js
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
// server/services/githubService.js
const https = require('https');

class GitHubService {
    constructor() {
        this.token = null;
        this.repo = null;
        this.owner = null;
        this.repoName = null;
        this.apiBase = 'api.github.com';
    }

    setCredentials(token, repo) {
        this.token = token;
        this.repo = repo;
        
        // Parse owner/repo format
        const parts = repo.split('/');
        if (parts.length !== 2) {
            throw new Error('Repository must be in format "owner/repo"');
        }
        this.owner = parts[0];
        this.repoName = parts[1];
    }

    isConnected() {
        return !!(this.token && this.repo && this.owner && this.repoName);
    }

    // Make authenticated request to GitHub API
    async request(path, method = 'GET', data = null) {
        return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
            const options = {
                hostname: this.apiBase,
                path: path,
                method: method,
                headers: {
                    'Authorization': `Bearer ${this.token}`,
                    'Accept': 'application/vnd.github+json',
                    'User-Agent': 'MT-Git-Manager/1.0',
                    'X-GitHub-Api-Version': '2022-11-28'
                }
            };

            if (data) {
                options.headers['Content-Type'] = 'application/json';
            }

            const req = https.request(options, (res) => {
                let body = '';
                res.on('data', chunk => body += chunk);
                res.on('end', () => {
                    try {
                        const parsed = JSON.parse(body);
                        if (res.statusCode >= 200 && res.statusCode < 300) {
                            resolve(parsed);
                        } else {
                            reject(new Error(parsed.message || `HTTP ${res.statusCode}`));
                        }
                    } catch (e) {
                        reject(new Error('Invalid JSON response'));
                    }
                });
            });

            req.on('error', (err) => reject(err));

            if (data) {
                req.write(JSON.stringify(data));
            }
            
            req.end();
        });
    }

    async validateConnection(token, repo) {
        // Temporarily set credentials for validation
        const prevToken = this.token;
        const prevRepo = this.repo;
        
        this.token = token;
        this.repo = repo;
        const parts = repo.split('/');
        this.owner = parts[0];
        this.repoName = parts[1];
        
        try {
            const result = await this.request(`/repos/${this.owner}/${this.repoName}`);
            return result;
        } catch (error) {
            // Restore previous credentials on failure
            this.token = prevToken;
            this.repo = prevRepo;
            this.owner = null;
            this.repoName = null;
            throw error;
        }
    }

    async listContents(path = '') {
        const url = `/repos/${this.owner}/${this.repoName}/contents/${path}?ref=main`;
        const data = await this.request(url);
        
        // Handle both array (directory) and object (single file) responses
        const items = Array.isArray(data) ? data : [data];
        
        return items.map(item => ({
            name: item.name,
            type: item.type === 'dir' ? 'directory' : 'file',
            path: item.path,
            sha: item.sha,
            size: item.size || 0,
            download_url: item.download_url,
            html_url: item.html_url
        }));
    }

    async getFileContent(path) {
        const url = `/repos/${this.owner}/${this.repoName}/contents/${path}?ref=main`;
        const data = await this.request(url);
        
        if (data.content) {
            // Decode base64 content
            return Buffer.from(data.content, 'base64').toString('utf-8');
        }
        
        throw new Error('No content in response');
    }

    async getFileInfo(path) {
        const url = `/repos/${this.owner}/${this.repoName}/contents/${path}?ref=main`;
        return await this.request(url);
    }

    async createFile(path, content, message) {
        const url = `/repos/${this.owner}/${this.repoName}/contents/${path}`;
        
        // Encode content to base64
        const encodedContent = Buffer.from(content).toString('base64');
        
        const data = {
            message: message,
            content: encodedContent,
            branch: 'main'
        };

        return await this.request(url, 'PUT', data);
    }

    async updateFile(path, content, sha, message) {
        const url = `/repos/${this.owner}/${this.repoName}/contents/${path}`;
        
        const encodedContent = Buffer.from(content).toString('base64');
        
        const data = {
            message: message,
            content: encodedContent,
            sha: sha,
            branch: 'main'
        };

        return await this.request(url, 'PUT', data);
    }

    async deleteFile(path, sha, message) {
        const url = `/repos/${this.owner}/${this.repoName}/contents/${path}`;
        
        const data = {
            message: message,
            sha: sha,
            branch: 'main'
        };

        return await this.request(url, 'DELETE', data);
    }

    async listBranches() {
        const url = `/repos/${this.owner}/${this.repoName}/branches`;
        return await this.request(url);
    }
}

module.exports = new GitHubService();
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/gitm/server/services/githubService.js.bak
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
const https = require('https');

class GitHubService {
    constructor() {
        this.token = null;
        this.repo = null;
        this.owner = null;
        this.repoName = null;
        this.apiBase = 'api.github.com';
    }

    setCredentials(token, repo) {
        this.token = token;
        this.repo = repo;
        
        // Parse owner/repo format
        const parts = repo.split('/');
        if (parts.length !== 2) {
            throw new Error('Repository must be in format "owner/repo"');
        }
        this.owner = parts[0];
        this.repoName = parts[1];
    }

    isConnected() {
        return !!(this.token && this.repo && this.owner && this.repoName);
    }

    // Make authenticated request to GitHub API
    async request(path, method = 'GET', data = null) {
        return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
            const options = {
                hostname: this.apiBase,
                path: path,
                method: method,
                headers: {
                    'Authorization': `Bearer ${this.token}`,
                    'Accept': 'application/vnd.github+json',
                    'User-Agent': 'MT-Git-Manager/1.0',
                    'X-GitHub-Api-Version': '2022-11-28'
                }
            };

            if (data) {
                options.headers['Content-Type'] = 'application/json';
            }

            const req = https.request(options, (res) => {
                let body = '';
                res.on('data', chunk => body += chunk);
                res.on('end', () => {
                    try {
                        const parsed = JSON.parse(body);
                        if (res.statusCode >= 200 && res.statusCode < 300) {
                            resolve(parsed);
                        } else {
                            reject(new Error(parsed.message || `HTTP ${res.statusCode}`));
                        }
                    } catch (e) {
                        reject(new Error('Invalid JSON response'));
                    }
                });
            });

            req.on('error', (err) => reject(err));

            if (data) {
                req.write(JSON.stringify(data));
            }
            
            req.end();
        });
    }

    async validateConnection(token, repo) {
        // Temporarily set credentials for validation
        const prevToken = this.token;
        const prevRepo = this.repo;
        
        this.token = token;
        this.repo = repo;
        const parts = repo.split('/');
        this.owner = parts[0];
        this.repoName = parts[1];
        
        try {
            const result = await this.request(`/repos/${this.owner}/${this.repoName}`);
            return result;
        } catch (error) {
            // Restore previous credentials on failure
            this.token = prevToken;
            this.repo = prevRepo;
            this.owner = null;
            this.repoName = null;
            throw error;
        }
    }

    async listContents(path = '') {
        const url = `/repos/${this.owner}/${this.repoName}/contents/${path}?ref=main`;
        const data = await this.request(url);
        
        // Handle both array (directory) and object (single file) responses
        const items = Array.isArray(data) ? data : [data];
        
        return items.map(item => ({
            name: item.name,
            type: item.type === 'dir' ? 'directory' : 'file',
            path: item.path,
            sha: item.sha,
            size: item.size || 0,
            download_url: item.download_url,
            html_url: item.html_url
        }));
    }

    async getFileContent(path) {
        const url = `/repos/${this.owner}/${this.repoName}/contents/${path}?ref=main`;
        const data = await this.request(url);
        
        if (data.content) {
            // Decode base64 content
            return Buffer.from(data.content, 'base64').toString('utf-8');
        }
        
        throw new Error('No content in response');
    }

    async getFileInfo(path) {
        const url = `/repos/${this.owner}/${this.repoName}/contents/${path}?ref=main`;
        return await this.request(url);
    }

    async createFile(path, content, message) {
        const url = `/repos/${this.owner}/${this.repoName}/contents/${path}`;
        
        // Encode content to base64
        const encodedContent = Buffer.from(content).toString('base64');
        
        const data = {
            message: message,
            content: encodedContent,
            branch: 'main'
        };

        return await this.request(url, 'PUT', data);
    }

    async updateFile(path, content, sha, message) {
        const url = `/repos/${this.owner}/${this.repoName}/contents/${path}`;
        
        const encodedContent = Buffer.from(content).toString('base64');
        
        const data = {
            message: message,
            content: encodedContent,
            sha: sha,
            branch: 'main'
        };

        return await this.request(url, 'PUT', data);
    }

    async deleteFile(path, sha, message) {
        const url = `/repos/${this.owner}/${this.repoName}/contents/${path}`;
        
        const data = {
            message: message,
            sha: sha,
            branch: 'main'
        };

        return await this.request(url, 'DELETE', data);
    }

    async listBranches() {
        const url = `/repos/${this.owner}/${this.repoName}/branches`;
        return await this.request(url);
    }
}

module.exports = new GitHubService();
```
